133(po)003	rgyal bstan snga 'gyur bka' ma theg rim dgu'i phrin chog gzhung phyi mo rnams dang bcas pa'i dkar chag bstan pa rgya mtsho'i gru gzings bkra shis dpal brgya'i 'byung gnas/	133	Thub bstan bshad bsgrub rgya mtsho		145	450	zhes pa 'di ni skyabs rje yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag mkhyen sprul rin po che 'jam dbyangs chos kyi blo gros ris med bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gang gi zhal snga nas bka' stsal spyi bor phebs pa dang | mchog sprul rin po che mdo sngags bstan pa'i nyi mas bka'i gnang ba stsal ba gus pas dang du blang ste rje bla ma o rgyan mdo sngags chos kyi nyi ma phyogs las rnam par rgyal ba'i sde dpal bzang po'i zhabs rdul spyi bos reg pa'i slob 'bangs yongs kyi tha shal du gyur pa sh+AAkya'i dge slong rmong rtul 'jam dbyangs thub bstan bshad sgrub rgya mtshor 'bod pas rang gnas dben pa'i ri sul du bkod pa dge legs 'phel ||
